    SELECT c."Id", c."CreatedAt", c."Description", c."Domain", c."InstructorId", c."IsDeleted", c."Language", c."Level", c."Price", c."Tags", c."ThumbnailUrl", c."Title", c."UpdatedAt", u."Id" AS "Id0", u."Bio", u."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", u."Email", u."FullName", u."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", u."PasswordHash", u."PhoneNumber", u."ProfilePictureUrl", u."RefreshToken", u."RefreshTokenExpiryTime", u."RoleId", u."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", u."Username"
